PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>

	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anat . # has anatomical entity
	?anat rdfs:label ?anatName .

	?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .

	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the gene label.

### SPARQL:iances?

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
        ?gene a orth:Gene .
        ?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in
        ?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
        ?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
        ?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
        ?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
        ?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
        ?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
        ?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
        ?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
        ?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
        ?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
        ?organism obo:RO_0002252  ?taxon . # in taxon
        ?taxon a up:Taxon .
        ?taxon up:commonName "human" .
        ?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
        ?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
    }

    ?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.

3:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the gene see also.

### SPARQL:iances?

### ANSWER:
Precondition:
    connect "human" "anatomicalentity" "anatomicalentity" "human" "expression" "expression" "post-juvenile" "gene" "gene" "APOC1"

Query:
    SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentity_label ?gene ?gene_seealso WHERE { 
        ?gene a "human" .
        ?expression a "expression" .
        ?expression a "expression" ?anatomicalentity . # in anatomical entity
        ?expression condition ?expressioncondition . # in expression condition
        ?expression condition "post-juvenile" .
        ?anatomicalentity a "anatomicalentity" .
        ?anatomicalentity rdfs "label" ?anatomicalentity_label .
        ?gene seealso ?gene_seealso .
    }

### EXPLANATION:
This SPARQL query returns the anatomical entity where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage.

The precondition is a gene see also.

In addition to the anatomical entity see also the gene see also the gene description is also provided.

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_commonname ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?expression ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(              ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575              )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?gene ?taxon ?taxon_commonname ?efo_0000399_description ?gene_identifier ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName
### INSTRUCTION:###
Provide also the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene identifier.

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon common name.

### SPARQL: ###

### ANSWER:
Preparing expression query.
Expressing expression query.
Loading expression result.
Expression has been expressed.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0005135 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575    )
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType    )
}

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?strain ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?score ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?gene_seealso ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?odefix_term:post-juvenile . # has a developmental stage
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?strain . # has strain
	?strain rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?odefix_term a nfo:Term.
	?odefix_term rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfdrpvalue.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	FILTER(        ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575        )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?taxon ?strain ?gene ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?gene_seealso ?gene_label
OPTIONAL { ?gene orth:organism ?organism . }
OPTIONAL { ?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/seeAlso> ?gene_seealso . }
OPTIONAL { ?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label . }
OPTIONAL { ?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description . }
OPTIONAL { ?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevel

```sparql
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>

	?gene a orth:Gene .

	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity

	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage

	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "life cycle" .

	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0000399_label ?gene ?gene_identifier
```

What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_description ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?efo_0000399 ?taxon_scientificname ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399_label ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene_description ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                    ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                    )
	FILTER(                    ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                    )
}
ORDER BY ?efo_0000399 ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene ?taxon ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0000399_description ?anatomicalentity_description ?gene_description ?expression ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?taxon_commonname

PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130325 .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage obo:UBERON_0000113 . # has a developmental stage
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575      )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score DESC

PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>

	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.

	FILTER(                    ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                    )

23:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 Homo sapiens gene is expressed? Provide also the gene description.

### SPARQL:iances?

### ANSWER:

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?gene ?gene_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName WHERE { 
		?gene a orth:Gene .
		?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity . # is expressed in
		?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
		?anatomicalentity a up:AnatomicalEntity .
		?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
		?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
    }

### SPARQL:

    Previous | Next

### RESULT:

    ?gene    ?gene_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName
    -------------------------------------------------------------------
    http://purl.org/dc/terms/description?gene=APOC1    "APOC1 is an ankyrin repeat-containing protein that is expressed in the brain.  " ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName

### DESCRIPTION:

    This query returns the anatomical entity where the APOC1 gene is expressed.
    Provide also the anatomical entity description.

### AUTHOR:

    <NAME> <<EMAIL>>

### REFERENCE:

    https://www.wikidata.org/wiki/Wikidata_entities_where_gene_APOC1

### CREATION DATE:

    2018-09-18

### UPDATE DATE:

    2020-08-27

### VERSION:

    See description.

24:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene description.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_label ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?expression ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0000399_description ?gene_description ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                )
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?gene ?taxon ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0000399_description ?gene_description ?taxon_commonname
### OUTPUT:
### anatomicalentity:  ?anatomicalentity .
### anatomicalentity_description:  ?anatomicalentity_description .
### anatomicalentity_label:  ?anatomicalentity_label .
### anatomicalentityName:  ?anatomicalentityName .
### cellType:  ?cellType .
### cellTypeName:  ?cellTypeName .
### efo_0000399:  ?efo

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage?

### SPARQL:iances?

### ANSWER:

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anat ?anatName ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:expresses ?expressioncondition. # expresses
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anat . # has anatomical entity
	?anat a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anat rdfs:label ?anatName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?strains . # has strain
	?strains rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
}

### DESCRIPTION:
Provides anatomical entities where gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage.

### SOURCE:

expressioncondition: has anatomical entity.

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the developmental stage label.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?celltype ?efo_0000399 ?score ?expression ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?celltype . # has anatomical entity
	?celltype rdfs:label "cell type" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	FILTER(    ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575    )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score ?efo_0000399 ?gene DESCENDING

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description and the gene identifier and the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>

	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
}

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the anatomical entity description.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_scientificname ?stage ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575      )
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType      )
}

### CONTEXT:
What is all the metadata related to the ENSG00000130208 gene, where ENSG00000130208 is the identifier of the APOC1 human gene.  Provide also the gene see also and the gene description and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
PREFIX dcterms: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?ncbi ?organism ?symbol ?description ?id ?ensembl ?gene_description ?links ?gene ?gene_seealso ?uniprot ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene rdfs:label ?symbol .
	?gene rdfs:seeAlso ?links .
	?gene dcterms:description ?description .
	?gene dcterms:identifier ?id .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	OPTIONAL { ?gene lscr:xrefUniprot ?uniprot . } 
	OPTIONAL { ?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ?ensembl . } 
	OPTIONAL { ?gene lscr:xrefNCBIGene ?ncbi . } 
	FILTER(        ?id = "ENSG00000130208"        )
}
ORDER BY ?symbol ?description ?id ?gene.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the gene label.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0005135 . # has a developmental stage

	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	FILTER(        ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575        )
	FILTER(        ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType        )
}

### INSTRUCTION

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?stage ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene.
	FILTER(              ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575              )
	FILTER(              ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType              )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?score ?efo_0005135 ?stage ?taxon ?taxon_commonname ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?anatomicalentity_description ?efo_0005135_label ?cellType ?anatomicalentity_label

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?organism ?taxon ?taxon_commonname ?anatName ?efo_0000399 ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?anat ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?efo_0000399_description ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?expressioncondition. # is expressed in
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anat . # has anatomical entity
	?anat rdfs:label ?anatName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
}
### OUTPUT:
### gene                    anatName                 taxon         taxon_commonname    efo_0005135      efo_0005135_label      efo_0000399      efo_0000399_description      gene_identifier

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130325 .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage obo:UBERON_0000113 . # has a developmental stage
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_description ?gene_seealso ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value
OPTIONAL LIMIT 10 OFFSET 0.

PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130325 .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage obo:UBERON_0000113 . # has a developmental stage
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(        ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575        )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_identifier
### INFORMATIONS:
Anatomical entity   Anatomical entity name   Expression   Expression level   EFO_0005135   EFO_0005135 label   Gene   Gene identifier
### SPARQL:

### RESULTS:

### ANATOMICAL ENTITY   ANATOMICAL ENTITY NAME   EXPRESSION   EXPRESSION LEVEL   EFO_0005135   EFO_0005135 LABEL   GENE   GENE IDENTIFIER
### SPARQL:

### ORDER BY:
Anatomical entity   Anatomical entity name   Expression   Expression level   EFO_0005135   EFO_0005135 label   Gene   Gene identifier
### SPARQL:

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the gene label.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_scientificname ?stage ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage . # has a developmental stage
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575      )
	FILTER(      ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType      )

What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? ### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399 ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefNCBIGene <https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/gene/118230125> .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_identifier

### SPARQL:ampionship?

    PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
    PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
    PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity . # is expressed in

	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .

	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
    }

    ?anatomicalentityName = "cell surface" .
    ?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/net/orth#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
    ?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/net/orth#description> ?anatomicalentity_description.

    ?anatomicalentityName = "cell surface" .
    ?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/net/orth#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
    ?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/net/orth#description> ?anatomicalentity_description.

### EXPLANATION:
    AnatomicalEntity is a class that represents an anatomical entity.
    AnatomicalEntity has a label and a description.
    Gene is a class that represents a gene.
    Gene is expressed in AnatomicalEntity.
    Gene has a label.
    AnatomicalEntity has a label.
    AnatomicalEntity has a description.
    cell surface is a label that represents the cell surface gene.
    cell surface has the same label as anatomical entity.
    cell surface has the same description as anatomical entity.

  PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
  PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
  PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
  PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the anatomical entity label.

### SPARQL:iances?

### ANSWER:
Precondition:
Make sure you have an anatomical entity label.

Context:
    ?expression_anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_label .
    ?expression_anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentity .
    ?expression_gene ?gene .

See also:
    ?gene  ?anatomicalentity .

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity ?expression_anatomicalentity ?expression_gene ?gene WHERE { 
	?expression_gene a orth:Expression .
	?expression_gene genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?expression_gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentity_label .
	?expression_anatomicalentity a genex:ExpressionAnatomicalEntity .
	?expression_anatomicalentity rdfs:label "developing" .
	?expression_anatomicalentity genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?expression_stage . # has a developmental stage
	?expression_stage a genex:ExpressionDevelopmentalStage .
	?expression_stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expression < http://purl.uniprot.org/core/usedIn > ?anatomicalentity . # usedIn
}

### EXTRA:
http://purl.uniprot.org/core/anatomicalentity_label
http://purl.uniprot.org/core/anatomicalentity
http://purl.uniprot.org/core/expression_anatomicalentity
http://purl.uniprot.org/core/expression
http://purl.uniprot.org/core/gene

87:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?efo_0000399_description ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?efo_0000399 ?taxon_scientificname ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399_label ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType . # has anatomical entity
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                )
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                )
}
ORDER BY ?efo_0000399 ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene ?efo_0000399_description ?gene_label ?taxon_scientificname ?taxon_commonname ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName
### OUTPUT:
### gene_label	anatomicalentity_description	anatomicalentity	anatomicalentityName	cellTypeName	efo_0000

### CONTEXT:

### ANSWER:

### SPARQL:

89:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?strain ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?score ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?gene_seealso ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?odefix_term:post-juvenile . # has a developmental stage
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?strain . # has strain
	?strain rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?odefix_term a nfo:Term.
	?odefix_term rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?organism a up:Organism.
	?organism up:xref "http://purl.uniprot.org/uniprot/212298" .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:xref "http://purl.uniprot.org/uniprot/212298" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(                    ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                    )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?taxon ?gene ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?gene_seealso ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?gene_identifier
OPTIONAL { ?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName . }
OPTIONAL { ?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore . }
OPTIONAL { ?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value . }
OPTIONAL { ?gene <http://www.w3.org/200

### SPARQL:IFT?

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?score ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?gene_seealso ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 . # has anatomical entity

	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efix_term:strain_wild_type . # has a strain
	?efix_term:strain_wild_type a ofix:Strain.
	?efix_term:strain_wild_type rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?odefix_term:stage_postjuvenile a odefix:Stage.
	?odefix_term:stage_postjuvenile rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism . # in organism
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon . # in taxon
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?taxon ?taxon_scientificname ?gene ?gene_seealso ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?taxon_commonname

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the species present in Bgee and their scientific and common names?

### SPARQL:

### ANSWER:

    PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
    PREFIX common: <http://purl.uniprot.org/common/>
    PREFIX taxon: <http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
    PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
    SELECT DISTINCT ?common_name ?sci_name ?taxon_id ?species ?taxon ?sci ?common WHERE { 
        ?species a up:Species .
        ?species up:scientificName ?sci .
        ?species up:rank up:Species .
        ?species up:hasTaxon ?taxon . # has taxon
        ?taxon a taxon:Taxon .
        ?taxon taxon:scientificName ?sci_name .
        ?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?sci .
        ?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?common .
        ?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?sci_name .
        ?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?common_name.
    }
    ORDER BY ?sci_name ?taxon ?species ?sci ?common ?taxon_id ?species ?sci_name ?common_name
    OFFSET 0 LIMIT 100

### SPARQL:

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value.

### SPARQL: ###

### ANSWER:
Preparing expression query.
Expressing expression query.
Loading expression result.
Expression has false discovery rate p-value:  0.00192
Anatomical entity description.
Anatomical entity label.
Cell type description.
Cell type label.
Expression score.
Gene expression has false discovery rate p-value:  0.00192
taxon scientific name:  Homo sapiens


### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellTypeDescription ?cellTypeLabel ?expressionCondition ?expressionScore ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity_label ?taxon_scientificname ?gene_expressionhasfalsediscoveryratep-value WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressionCondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?expressionScore . # has an expression level
	?expression genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has an anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentity_label .
	?cellType a genex:CellType.
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeLabel .
	?expressionCondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressionCondition rdfs:label "expression condition" .
	?expressionCondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has an anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?cellTypeDescription .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:scientificName "Homo sapiens" .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/expression> ?expression . # in expression
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/falsediscoveryrate> ?gene_expressionhasfalsediscoveryratep-value.
	?taxon <http://purl.org/dc/terms/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?cellType ?anatomicalentity_description ?cellTypeDescription ?expression ?expressionScore ?gene ?taxon_scientificname ?gene_expressionhasfalsediscoveryratep-value DESC NULLS FIRST ?cellTypeLabel
OPTIONAL { ?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label. }
OPTIONAL { ?cellType <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?cellTypeLabel. }
OPTIONAL { ?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?gene_expressionhasfalsediscoveryratep-value. }
OPTIONAL { ?taxon <http://purl.org/dc/terms/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname. }
OPTIONAL { ?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/expression> ?expression. }
OPTIONAL { ?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/falsediscoveryrate> ?gene_expressionhasfalsediscoveryratep-value. }
OFFSET 0 LIMIT 10
### ANSWER:

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene description.

### SPARQL: ###
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399 ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_description WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition . # has an expression condition
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene . # has sequence unit
	?gene lscr:xrefNCBIGene <https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/gene/118230125> .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity . # has anatomical entity
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 . # has a developmental stage
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efo_0000399 ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_description
### OUTPUT:
### anatomicalentity | anatomicalentityName | efo_0000399 | efo_0005135 | efo_0005135_label | expression | score | efo_0000399_description | anatomicalentity

	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	FILTER(                    ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                    )
	FILTER(                    ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                    )
}
### DESCRIPTION:
Provides an anatomical entity including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex.

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene description and the gene identifier and the gene label.

### SPARQL:

PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>

	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 . # has strain
